< Review>
Uniformly poor service and support all the way around.  Their response? "We've been doing this for 82 years and know better than you!"

Lawrance neither understands nor practices the basics of retailing. They should know consumers expect:

Convenience
Confidence and Trust in their purchases
Support
Value

I ordered replacement parts for two Trica lamps stocked by this retailer. Lawrance refused to take the $75 order over the phone and made me drive to their store to make the purchase.

Next, I was told to expect delivery in a matter of days.  Two weeks later I have received nothing and my calls to Lawrance went unanswered. They never bothered to keep that one simple promise - to call me back with the status of an order.

However, that is not to say you cannot get Lawrance to to be responsive to customer issues. Apparently, their social media review department is always open and always vigilant for negative reviews such as this one here.

Unable to get any kind of update on my order, the heir-apparent of the Lawrance legacy, Joel Haimsohn, text messaged me immediately after this review was posted (late Friday eve) and called me the following day.

Not only did Mr. Haimsohn not take responsibility for his failure, he cravenly blamed the Trica Furniture rep and in his own words, Haimsohn "threw him under the bus."  Actually, the Trica factory rep was the ONLY person that responded to my inquiries whereas Lawrance never returned my calls.

Mr. Haimsohn defended the store's policy of not taking phone orders and forcing their customers to drive to their brick-and-mortar location to order spare parts for the lines they carry.  His reason?  His mother ran the business for 82 years and 20 years ago decided Lawrance was not taking any phone orders due to the threat of fraud.  Apparently, I underestimated the scope of fraud rings preying upon furniture stores with fraudulent lamp cord orders.

It is that kind of ephemeral thinking that got Sears, JC Penny and a thousand other retailers their well-deserved place in the dustbin of history.

Why would you want to purchase anything from a high-end furniture retailer that blithely disregards their customers and forces them to schlep to the store for trivial replacement/service parts and then blames any errant happenings on outsiders?

This place caters to the interior design trade and fares rather poorly as a retailer.< /Review>

< Review>
Blown away. The reviews weren't kidding when they said it was a little hard to find, but the Black Fig is inside the Psi-Arc architecture school across the street from the cafes and shops on Santa Fe. Once you find your way inside, ask for directions and they'll point you the right way. The prices are pretty good and they've got a wide variety of options for salads and sandwiches. Their best food however is the burgers. 10/10 would come back if I'm in the area and in the mood for a quick meal.<//Review>

<text>I was on a long drive for work when a coworker and I decided to stop in here for dinner before continuing on our way. The place is a bit run down looking from the street but don't let that fool you or stop you. Inside, this hole in the wall has character in the decor, and a fenced off outside seating area out a side door.

The prices are a bit high, but the pizza is great! Not oily, the dough and veggies are fresh, and it's delicious. We couldn't indulge due to driving and being on the job, also I'm not a beer person... but this place also serves beer. The kitchen equipment is visible from the service counter and it's no Dave Ramsey kitchen as the equipment is older and seen years of use, but it's tidy and clean.

Was here yesterday. Note for some reviews they are talking about the massage, and others just about the bath house. Two different things. I didn't get a massage, nor do you have to to go and experience it. If you love Saunas and a super clean and friendly staff (shorter girl with dark hair that works there is very friendly) then check it out. I thought it was absolutely awesome and a legit perfect way to spend some money.

As far as COVID. I went mid week mid morning and I had saunas and even the baths to myself. It was easy to avoid being close to people and spread out / wear masks.

Overall 10/10 and really what more could you ask for? Saunas, showers, warm pools, cold dip, lawn chairs to soak in some sun in between saunas.< /review>

<user_id>108891062784388095914</user_id><rate>5</rate>< review>
I'm so glad this place exists in Sacramento. When I was in Japan, I developed a bit of a public bath fixation. And this place really draws from that tradition. The facilities are very clean and well maintained, everyone there is very nice and respectful. Overall, it's a relaxing and enjoyable place to be. There is a large, warm soaking pool. It's not as hot as most hot tubs, so you can sit in it longer without feeling like you're going to pass out. There is a steam room and a sauna. And also a cold dip pool, which is my favorite part. Taking a cold dip after getting hot in the sauna is the best. If you're curious, you really should give this place a shot. You might just like it.<//review>

<review>oh my goodness...Chef Brian, open up one of these in the NW please!!

I dined here while visiting Fountain Valley on a work trip. After our training, 10 of us came to Tackle Box around 5pm. Most of us were from out of the town, but for the handful of locals it was also their first time here.

I don‚Äôt know how to explain but it‚Äôs kind of; fast-casual-local-fresh-innovative? lol. You order at the counter and seat yourself. There are at least 2 that I saw, water stations, so you can help yourself. After ordering a drink at the counter, they bring it to you.

The interior is bright, and exciting and comfortable. There is some outdoor seating as well as low and high seating inside. The 10 of us were able to fit at one long high table.

We ordered for the table; chips and salsa (homemade chips and super fresh, light salsa), grilled half artichoke (not much meat on the leaves but amazing flavor!), wings (crispy, juicy, tender, everything you want in a wing), and baby back ribs (fall off the bone tender!).

I had a hard time choosing what to order as literally the entire menu looked appealing! I eventually settled on the fried catfish sandwich, Y U M! Perfectly crispy cornmeal fried catfish which was moist and flavorful, fresh tomato and shredded lettuce, vinegary remoulade that packed a punch!, and soft yet somehow also firm bread that held together all of the goodness! The homemade chips were awesome, and I‚Äôm always a fan of the addition of a pickle spear ;)

10/10 would recommend you try Tackle box!!< /review></record></dataset><record>

< Review>
I came here for my first time today on the recommendation of a friend. I beat him there so I grabbed a beer and sat out on the patio. The beer selection is excellent! When he arrived, I placed my order for a chicken club sandwich with avocado and added another beer on for when I finished my first.

The food came out quickly and was delicious! The chicken was perfectly seasoned and all of the flavors went together very well! The sandwich comes with house chips which are season deliciously (Old Bay I think)!  Right when I was finishing up my first beer, the second one came out without me asking! It was awesome that they were paying attention to the patio enough to catch the small details like that.

Overall the food and service were both excellent. I will definitely be coming back soon.<//Review>

< review>
First time getting wings from this restaurant.  The online ordering experience was quick and easy.  The price was reasonable.  Picking up the order was also quick with a friendly staff.  The wings, traditional wings with Buffalo medium hot sauce, did not meet my expectation.  I ate tons of wings when I went to school in Buffalo, NY and this was not it..

Update 7/24.  Take-out service was friendly and quick.  After I get home I found that the celery and carrots were missing.  I ordered with sauce on the side and I liked it better this way.  3 stars.

Update 8/20.  Take-out service was friendly and quick again.  The celery and carrots were in the bag.  I ordered with the sauce on the side.  The wings were really dry this time.  Back to 2 stars.

If you wondered why I kept going back since I thought the wings were mediocre.  Well, cause I have a $100 gift card that I want to use up.  Maybe I should order something other than the wings next time?</review>

< time>
1502690030590< /time>
<rating>4</rating>< Review>
I only go on Tuesdays, so this review is only for Tuesday nights... for the inexpensive wings. They are great. The onion rings are also the best I've had anywhere. But this is also when everyone else wants cheap wings, and this location has not figured out how to deal with the demand, especially when a game is on (it gets very loud too). Not sure who is to blame, but the wait time to be seated is about 30 minutes on average after 7pm, and after you order your food it takes another 30 minues to an hour for it to come out of the kitchen. Granted, they do warn you about the wait ahead of time. Ive started to order the wings to-go, and giving myself an hour before I leave to pick them up. It seems like many people have started doing this as well since the wait times for to-go orders have been increasing. Maybe some day they'll figure out a way to work the crowds. It's my favorite wing place! But make sure you have some time to spend.< /Review>

< name>
Evelynn Chiu< /name>
< text>
Surprisingly, my most recent experience at BWW greatly surpassed my expectations in terms of service. Our waitress was friendly and to be honest, I thought she was pretty cool. 4 minutes before happy hour ended, we reached out for her attention and told her we were trying to squeeze in our drink orders before happy hour ended, she understood fully and made it her mission. She came back with a grin on her face and told us we're set and then proceeded to take our orders. Not too long later, the food came out and she left us to it, checking up on us once or twice. "Do you guys need anything....*scans the table for a second* you need napkins!"

Her service alone deserves 5 stars, but if I'm being completely honest, the past couple times I've been here had subpar and spotty service. Not to mention, I'm really reviewing the food here right?

FOOD:
Boneless -- Extremely dry, tough pieces of chicken.. They weren't even warm. Nearly $10 for a snack size??? I could have bought a large bag from the grocery store and microwaved it for that price and it would still taste better.. Disappointing.

Traditional Wings -- It seemed like my friends really enjoyed their half off deal. $10 for a large size (20 pieces) of wings was not a bad deal.

Basket of fries -- the highlight of my meal personally... Seasoned with buffalo dry-rub and freshly fried, these were good. Unfortunately the spices built up in my mouth quickly and I was too *chicken* (hehe..) to continue my quest in finishing it. On the bright side, I REALLY enjoyed my Racer 5 IPA because of it.

BWW is a good place to catch up with friends over some drinks, but pick and choose your time wisely or you'll end up waiting a long time for a spot when you can just go elsewhere. Experience is entirely based on who you get as your waiter/waitress. Food is nothing special.< /text>
